<p>The leading European teams, <a href="/dota2/Epic_Esports_Events" title="Epic Esports Events">Epic Esports Events</a> and <a href="/dota2/WePlay!" class="mw-redirect" title="WePlay!">WePlay! Esports</a> joined forces to host a new multi-level international Dota 2 league: <b>OMEGA League</b>, featuring divisions for Americas and Europe with a total prize pool of $600,000 <abbr title="United States Dollar">USD</abbr>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=OMEGA_League/1/Americas/Divine_Division&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Participants</b>
<ul><li>Six invited teams</li>
<li>Two teams from North America open qualifier</li>
<li>Two teams from South America open qualifier</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Group Stage</b> - <i>August 17th - August 27th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Two groups of five teams each</li>
<li>Single round-robin</li>
<li>All matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(221,244,221);">Top two teams</span> from each group advance to the Upper Bracket R1 of the Playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(249,222,199);">3<sup>rd</sup> and 4<sup>th</sup> place teams</span> from each group advance to the Play-in Stage to determine who advance to the Lower Bracket R1 of Playoffs, eliminated teams advance to Quarterfinals of the ancient division's Playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(251,223,223);">Bottom team</span> from each group advance to the Quarterfinals of the ancient division's Playoffs</li>
<li><span class="mw-customtoggle-Tiebreaker" style="border-bottom:1px dotted;"><i>Click here for tiebreaker rules</i></span></li></ul></li></ul>
<div class="toccolours mw-collapsible mw-collapsed" id="mw-customcollapsible-Tiebreaker" style="width:760px; margin-left:45px">
<ul><li>If two or more teams have an equal amount of points, the final standings will be ruled based on the following priority:
<ol><li>Number of matches won 2:0</li>
<li>Maps difference</li>
<li>The sum of series wins for all of the teams that tied teams beat</li>
<li>Head-to-head result</li></ol></li>
<li>Should the tie be broken for one of the tied teams, the same process will be repeated from priority 1 for the rest of the teams that are still tied.</li>
<li>If one or more of the tied teams should be eliminated - <abbr title="Best-of-one">Bo1</abbr> tiebreaker matches will be played till the tie is broken.</li></ul>
</div>
<ul><li><b>Playoffs</b> - <i>August 28th - September 5th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Double-elimination bracket</li>
<li>Grand Final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr>, all other matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>
